\subsubsection[{C\-H\-A\-N\-G\-E\-D\-\_\-\-C\-E\-L\-L}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define C\-H\-A\-N\-G\-E\-D\-\_\-\-C\-E\-L\-L(
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
\item[{}]{line, }
\item[{}]{col}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{curses_8priv_8h_a1d3a1639c7c2795f7b707c82e817e1b9}
{\bfseries Value\-:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
\textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (line->firstchar == \_NOCHANGE) \(\backslash\)
        line->firstchar = line->lastchar = (NCURSES\_SIZE\_T) (col); \(\backslash\)
    else \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((col) < line->firstchar) \(\backslash\)
        line->firstchar = (NCURSES\_SIZE\_T) (col); \(\backslash\)
    else \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((col) > line->lastchar) \(\backslash\)
        line->lastchar = (NCURSES\_SIZE\_T) (col)
\end{DoxyCode}
